Lekin woh log un se woh baate sikhte thay jis se miya-biwi ke darmiyaan jaghda kara de, haala ke izne Khuda ke ba-ghair woh kisi ko nuksaan nahi pohoncha sakte. yeh un se woh sab-kuch sikhte thay jo unke liye muzirr (Nuksaan deh) tha aur uska koi faaida nahi tha yeh khoob jaante thay ke jo bhi un cheezo ko khareedega uska aakherat mein koi hissa na hoga. Unho ne apne nafs ka bohot bura sauda kiya hai agar yeh kuch jaante aur samajh-te ho.

103. Agar yeh log imaan le aate aur muttaqi ban jaate to khudai sawaab bohot behtar tha, agar unki samajh mein aajaata.

104. Imaan waalo! “ra’ena” (hamaari re’aayat karo & other meaning) na kaha karo. “unzurna” (hamaari re’aayat karo) kaha karo aur ghaur se soona karo aur yaad rakkho ke kaafereen ke liye bada dard-naak azaab hai.

105. Kaafir Ahle kitaab yahood-o-nasaara aur aam mushreqeen yeh nahi chahte ke tumhaare upar Parwardigaar ki taraf se koi khair naazil ho haala keh Allah jise chahta hai apni rehmat ke liye makhsoos kar leta hai aur Allah bade fazl-o-karam ka maalik hai.

106. Aur ay Rasool ham jab bhi kisi ayat ko mansookh karte hai ya dilo se mahv kar dete hai to us se behtar ya uski jaisi ayat zaroor le aate hai. kya tum nahi jaante ke Allah har shaiy par qaadir hai.

107. Kya tum nahi jaante ke aasmaan-o-zameen ki hukumat sirf Allah ke liye hai aur iske alaawa koi sarparast hai na madad-gaar.

108. Ay logo! Kya tum yeh chahte ho ke apne Rasool se waisa hi mutaalba (sawaal) karo jaisa ke Moosa alayhis salaam se kiya gaya tha to yaad rakkho ke jisne imaan ko kufr se badal liya woh bad-tareen raaste par gumraah ho gaya hai.

109. Bohat se Ahle kitaab yeh chahte hai ke tumhe bhi imaan ke baad kaafir bana le woh tum se hasad rakhte hai warna haq un par bilkul waazeh hai to ab tum inhe maaf kar do aur un se darguzar karo yahan tak keh Khuda apna koi hukm bhej de aur Allah har shaiy par qaadir hai.

110. Aur tum namaaz qaayem karo aur zakaat adaa karo ke jo kuch apne waaste pehle bhej donge sab Khuda ke yahan mil jaayega. Khuda tumhaare aamaal ko khoob dekhne waala hai.

111. Yeh yahoodi kehte hai ke jannat mein yahoodiyo aur isaiyyo ke alaawa koi daakhil na hoga. yeh sirf unki ummeede hai. un se kahe dijiye keh agar tum sachche ho to koi daleel le aawo.

112. Nahi, jo shakhs apna rukh Khuda ki taraf kar dega aur nek amal karega uske liye Parwardigaar ke yahan ajr hai aur na koi khauf hai na huzn (gham).

113. Aur yahoodi kehte hai ke nasaara ka mazhab kuch nahi hai aur nasaara kehte hai ke yahoodiyo ki koi buniyaad nahi hai haala keh dono hi kitaabe ilaahi ki tilaawat karte hai aur iske pehle jaahil mushreqeen arab bhi yahi kaha karte thay. Khuda un sab ke darmiyaan roz-e-qayamat faisla karne waala hai.

114. Aur isse badh kar zaalim kaun hoga jo masjide Khuda mein uska naam lene se mana kare aur unki barbaadi ki koshish kare. Un logo ka hissa sirf yeh hai ke msajid mein khaufzada ho kar daakhil ho aur unke liye duniya mein ruswaee hai aur aakherat mein azaabe azeem.

115. Aur Allah ke liye mashriq bhi hai aur maghrib bhi lehaaza tum jis jagah bhi qible ka rukh kar loge samjho wahi Khuda maujood hai woh saahibe wus’at (Extent) bhi hai aur saahibe ilm bhi hai.

116. Aur yahoodi kehte hai ke Khuda ke aulaad bhi hai haala keh woh paak-o-be-niyaz hai. Zameen-o-aasmaan mein jo kuch bhi hai sab usi ka hai aur sab usi ke farmabardaar hai.

117. Woh zameen-o-aasmaan ka mujaad (banaane waala) hai aur jab kisi amr ka faisla kar leta hai to sirf “kun” (ho-jaa) kaheta hai aur woh cheez ho jaati hai.

118. Yeh jaahil mushreqeen kehte hai ke Khuda ham se kalaam kyu’n nahi karta aur ham par ayat kyu’n naazil nahi karta. Unke pehle waale bhi aisi hi jehaalat ki baate kar chuke hai. Un sab ke dil milte-julte hai aur ham ne to Ahle yaqeen ke liye aayaat ko waazeh kar diya hai.

119. Ay Paighambar ham ne aap ko haq ke saath bashaarat dene waala aur daraane waala bana kar bheja hai aur aap se Ahle jahannum ke baare mein koi sawaal na kiya jaayega.

120. Yahood-o-nasaara aap se us waqt tak raazi na hoge jab tak aap unki millat ki pairwi na kar le to aap kahe dijiye keh hidaayat sirf hidaayate parwar-digar hai. Aur agar aap ilm ke ane ke baad unki khwahishaat ki paherawi karege to phir Khuda ke azaab se bachaane waala na koi sarparast hoga na madadgar.

121. Aur jin logo ko ham ne qu’ran diya hai woh iski ba-qaaeda tilaawat karte hai aur unhi ka is par imaan bhi hai aur jo iska inkaar karega uska shumar khasaare (nuksaan) waalo mein hoga.

122. Ay bani Israeel un nemato ko yaad karo jo ham ne tumhe inaayat ki hai aur jin ke tufayl tumhe saare aalam se behtar bana diya hai.

123. Aur us din se daro jis din koi kisi ka fidya (ransom) na ho sakegha aur na koi muawza (badla) kaam aayega na koi sifarish hogi aur na koi madad ki ja sakegi.

124. Aur us waqt ko yaad karo jab Khuda ne chand kalemaat ke zariye Ibrahim alayhis salaam ka imtehaan liya aur unho ne pura kar diya to us ne kaha ke ham tum ko logo ka imam aur qaaed (leader) bana rahe hai. Unho ne arz ki ke meri zurriyat? Irshaad huwa ke yeh ohda-e-imamat zaalemeen tak nahi jaayega.

125. Aur us waqt ko yaad karo jab ham ne khana-e-kaaba ko sawaab aur aman ki jagah banaya aur hukm de diya ke maqame Ibrahim ko musalla banaawo aur Ibrahim alayhis salaam-o-Ismaeel alayhis salaam se ahed liya ke hamare ghar ko tawaf aur etekaaf karne waalo aur ruku-o-sajdah karne waalo ke liye paak-o-pakeeza banaaye rakkho.

126. Aur us waqt ko yaad karo jab Ibrahim alayhis salaam ne dua ki ke Parwardigaar is shaher ko amn ka shaher qaraar de-de aur iske un Ahle shaher ko jo Allah aur aakherat par imaan rakhte ho phalo ka rizq ataa farma. Irshaad huwa ke phir jo kaafir ho jaayege unhe duniya mein thodi nematein de kar aakherat mein azaab-e-Jahannam mein zabardasti dhakel diya (push kiya) jaayega jo badtareen anjaam hai.

127. Aur us waqt ko yaad karo jab Ibrahim alayhis salaam Ismaeel alyhis salaam khana-e-kaaba ki diwaaro ko buland kar rahe thay aur dil mein yeh dua thi ke Parwardigaar hamari mehnat ko qabool farma le ke tu behtareen soonne waala aur jaanne waala hai.

128. Parwardigaar ham dono ko apna musalmaan aur farma-bardaar (obedient) qaraar dede aur hamari aulaad mein bhi ek farma-bardaar (obedient) ummat paiyda kar. Hamein hamare manaasik (aamaal) dikhla de aur hamaari tauba qabool farma ke tu behtareen tauba qabool karne waala maher-baan hai.

129. Parwardigaar unke darmiyaan ek Rasool ko mab’oos (intekhaab) farma jo unke saamne Teri aayato ki tilaawat kare. unhe kitaab-o-hikmat ki taaleem de aur unke nafoos ko pakeeza banaaye. Be-shak tu sahib-e-izzat aur sahib-e-hikmat hai.

130. Aur kaun hai jo bhala Ibrahim alayhis salaam se earaz kare (phir jaaye) magar yeh ke apne hi ko be-waqoof banaaye. Aur ham ne unhe duniya mein muntakhab (select) qaraar diya hai aur woh aakherat mein nek kirdaar logo mein hai.

131. Jab un se unke Parwardigaar ne kaha ke apne ko mere hawaale kar do to unho ne kaha ke mein rabul alalmin ke liye saraapa tasleem (itaa’at karne waala) hu.

132. Aur isi baat ki Ibrahim alayhis salaam aur Yaqoob alayhis salaam ne apni aulaad ko wasiyat ki ke ay mere farzando Allah ne tumhaare liye deen ko muntakhab kar diya hai ab us waqt tak duniya se na jaana jab tak waaqeyi musalmaan na ho jaawo.

133. Kya tum us waqt tak maujood thay jab Yaqoob alayhis salaam ka waqte maut aaya aur unho ne apni aulaad se poocha ke mere baad kis ki ibaadat karoge to unho ne kaha ke aap ke aur aap ke abaao ajdaad Ibrahim alayhis salaam-o-Ismaeel alayhis salaam, Ishaaq alayhis salaam ke Parwardigaar Khuda e wahdahu la-sharik ki aur ham usi ke musalmaan aur farma-bardaar (obedient) hai.

134. Yahoodiyo! yeh qaum thi jo guzar gayi inhe woh milega jo unho ne kamaaya aur tumhe woh milega jo tum kamaawoge tum se unke aamaal ke baare mein sawaal na hoga.

135. Aur yeh yahoodi aur isaayi kehte hai ke tum log bhi yahoodiaur isaayi ho jaawo ta-keh hidaayat pa jaawo toaap kahe de ke sahih raasta baatil se katra kar chalne waale Ibrahim alayhis salaam ka raasta hai ke woh mushreqeen mein nahi thay.

136. Aur musalmaano! Tum un se kaho ke ham Allah par aur jo us ne hamari taraf bheja hai aur jo Ibrahim alayhis salaam, Ismaeel alayhis salaam, Ishaaq alayhis salaam, Yaqoob alayhis salaam, aulaade Yaqoob alayhis salaam ki taraf naazil kiya hai aur jo Moosa alayhis salaam, esa alayhis salaam aur ambiya alayhemus salaam ko Parwardigaar ki taraf se diya gaya hai un sab par imaan le aaye hai. Ham paighambaro alayhemus salaam mein tafreeq (farq) nahi karte aur ham Khuda ke sachche musalmaan hai.

137. Ab agar yeh log bhi aisa hi imaan le aayege to hidaayat yaafta ho jaayege aur agar earaz karege (phir jaayege) to yeh sirf enaad (na-farmaani) hoga aur an-qareeb Allah tumhe un sab ke shar se bacha lega keh woh soonne waala bhi hai aur janne waala bhi hai.

138. Rang to sirf Allah ka rang hai aur us se behtar kis ka rang ho sakta hai aur ham sab usi ke ibaadat-guzaar hai.

139. Ay Rasool kahe dijiye keh kya tum ham se us Khuda ke baare mein jagadte ho jo hamara bhi Parwardigaar hai aur tumhaara bhi, to hamare liye hamare aamaal hai aur tumhaare liye tumhaare aamaal aurham to sirf Khuda ke mukhlis bande hai.

140. Kya tumhaara kehna yeh hai ke Ibrahim alayhis salaam, Ismaeel alayhis salaam, Ishaaq alayhis salaam, Yaqoob alayhis salaam aur aulade Yaqoob alayhemus salaam yahoodi ya nasrani thay. To ay Rasool kahe dijiye keh kya tum Khuda se behtar jaante ho. Aur isse bada zaalim kaun hoga jiske paas khudai shahadat maujood ho aur woh phir parda-poshi kare aur Allah tumhaare aamaal se ghaafil nahi hai.

141. Yeh ummat guzar chuki hai uska hissa woh hai jo us ne kiya hai aur tumhaara hissa woh hai jo tum karoge aur Khuda tum se unke aamaal ke baare mein koi sawaal nahi karega.

142. An-qareeb ehmaq log yeh Kahenge keh in musalmaano ko us qible se kis ne moud diya hai jis par pehle qaayem thay to ay Paighambar kahe dijiye keh mashriq-o-maghrib sab Khuda ke hai woh jise chahta hai seraat-e-mustaqeem ki hidaayat de deta hai.

143. Aur tehweel-e-qibla ki tarah ham ne tum ko darmiyaani ummat qaraar diya hai ta-keh tum logo ke aamaal ke gawah raho aur Paighambar tumhaare aamaal ke gawah rahe aur Ham ne pehle qible ko sirf is liye qibla banaya tha keh Ham yeh dekhe ke kaun Rasool ka itteba karta hai aur kaun pichhle paau palat jaata hai. Agar-che yeh qibla sab par giran hai alaawa un logo ke jin ki Allah ne hidaayat kar di hai aur Khuda tumhaare imaan ko zaaya nahi karna chahta. Woh bando ke haal par maher-baan aur rahem karne waala hai.

144. Ay Rasool Ham aap ki tawajjo ko aasmaan ki taraf dekh rahe hai to Ham an-qareeb aap ko us qible ki taraf moud dege jise aap pasand karte hai lehaaza aap apna rukh masjidul haraam ki jehat ki taraf moud dijiye aur jahan bhi rahe isi taraf rukh kijiye. Ahle kitaab khoob jaante hai keh Khuda ki taraf se yahi bar-haq hai aur Allah un logo ke aamaal se ghaafil nahi hai.

145. Agar aap un Ahle kitaab ke paas tamaam aayate bhi pesh kar de keh yeh aap ke qibla ko maan le to harghiz na maanege aur aap bhi unke qible ko na maanege aur yeh aapas mein bhi ek dusre ke qible ko nahi maante aur ilm ke aa jaaane ke baad agar aap unki khwahishaat ka itteba kar lege to aap ka shumaar zaalimo mein ho jaayega.

146. Jin logo ko Ham ne kitaab di hai woh Rasool ko bhi apni aulaad ki tarah pehchaante hai. Bas unka ek giroh hai jo haq ko deeda-o-daanista (jaan-bujh kar) chhupa rahe hai.

147. Ay Rasool yeh haq aap ke Parwardigaar ki taraf se hai lehaaza aap un shak-o-shubhe karne waalo mein na ho jaaye.

148. Har ek ke liye ek rukh mo’ayyan hai aur woh usi ki taraf mooh karta hai. Ab tum nekiyo ki taraf sabqat karo aur tum sab jahan bhi rahoge Khuda ek din sab ko jama kar dega keh woh har shaiy par qaadir hai.

149. Paighambar aap jahan se baahar nikle apna rukh masjidul haraam ki simt hi rakkhe keh yahi Parwardigaar ki taraf se haq hai. Aur Allah tum logo ke aamaal se ghaafil nahi hai.

150. Aur aap jahan se bhi nikle apna rukh khaan-e-kaaba ki taraf rakkhe aur phir tum sab jahan raho tum sab bhi apna rukh idhar hi rakkho ta-keh logo ke liye tumhaare upar koi hujjat na rahe jaaye siwaaye un logo ke, keh jo zaalim hai to unka khauf na karo bal-keh Allah se daro keh Ham tum par apni nemat tamaam kar dena chahte hai keh shaayad tum hidaayat yaafta ho jaawo.

151. Jis tarah Ham ne tumhaare darmiyaan tum hi mein se ek Rasool bheja hai jo tum par hamari aayaat ki tilaawat karta hai tumhe paak-o-pakeeza banata hai aur tumhe kitaab-o-hikmat ki taaleem deta hai aur woh sab-kuch bataata hai jo tum nahi jaante thay.

152. Ab tum Ham ko yaad karo ta-keh ham tumhe yaad rakkhe aur hamara shukriya adaa karo aur kufraan-e-nemat na karo.

153. Imaan waalo! Sabr aur namaaz ke zariye madad maango ke Khuda sabr karne waalo ke saath hai.

154. Aur jo log raahe Khuda mein qatl ho jaate hai unhe murda na kaho bal-keh woh zinda hai lekin tumhe unki zindagi ka shaoor nahi hai.

155. Aur Ham yaqeenan tumhe thode khauf thodi bhookh aur amwal, nufoos aur samaraat ki kami se azmaayege aur ay Paighambar aap un sabr karne waalo ko bashaarat de-de.

156. Jo museebat padhne ke baad yeh kehte hai keh ham Allah hi ke liye hai aur usi ki baargah mein waapas jaane waale hai.

157. Keh unke liye Parwardigaar ki taraf se salwaat aur rehmat hai aur wohi hidaayat yaafta hai.

158. Be-shak Safa aur Marwa dono pahadiya Allah ki nishaniya mein hai lehaaza jo shakhs bhi hajj ya umrah kare uske liye koi harj nahi hai keh un dono pahadiyo ka chakkar lagaaye aur jo mazeed kher karega to Khuda uske amal ka qadr-daan aur us se khoob waaqif hai.

159. Jo log hamare naazil kiye huwe waazeh bayanaat aur hidaayat ko hamare bayaan kar dene ke baad bhi chhipate hai un par Allah bhi laanat karta hai aur tamaam laanat karne waale bhi laanat karte hai.

160. Alaawa un logo ke jo tauba kar le aur apne kiye ki islaah kar le aur jis ko chhupaya hai us ko waazeh kar de to ham unki tauba qabool kar lete hai ke ham behtareen tauba qabool karne waale aur maher-baan hai.

161. Jo log kaafir ho gaye aur usi haale kufr mein mar gaye un par Allah, malaayeka aur tamaam insaano ki laanat hai.

162. Woh usi laanat mein hamesha rahege keh na unke azaab mein takhfeef (kami) hogi aur na inhe mohlat di jaayega.

163. Aur tumhaara Khuda bas ek hai. uske alaawa koi Khuda nahi hai wohi Rehmaan bhi hai aur wohi Raheem bhi hai.

164. Be-shak zameen-o-aasmaan ki khilqat roz-o-shab ki raft-o-aamad (aana-jaana). Un kashtiyo mein jo dariyaao mein logo ke faaide ke liye chalti hai aur us paani mein jise Khuda ne aasmaan se naazil kar ke uske zariye murda zameeno ko zinda kar diya hai aur us mein tarah-tarah ke chopaaye phaila diye hai aur hawaao ke chalne mein aur aasmaan-o-zameen ke darmiyaan musakhkhar (stable) kiye jaane waale baadal mein sahebaan-e-aql ke liye Allah ki nishaaniya paayi jaati hai.

165. logo mein kuch aise log bhi hai jo Allah ke alaawa dusro ko uska misl qaraar dete hai aur un se Allah jaisi mohabbat bhi karte hai jab-keh imaan waalo ki tamaam-tar mohabbat Khuda se hoti hai aur ay kaash zaalemeen is baat ko us waqt dekh lete jo azaab ko dekhne ke baad samjhege ke saari quwwat sirf Allah ke liye hai aur Allah sakht-tareen azaab karne waala hai.

166. Us waqt jab-keh peer apne mureedo se be-zaari ka izhaar karege aur sab ke saamne azaab hoga aur tamaam wasaael munqata ho chuke hoge.

167. Aur mureed bhi yeh Kahenge keh ay kaash ham ne un se isi tarah be-zaari ikhtiyaar ki hoti jis tarah yeh aaj hamse nafrat kar rahe hai. Khuda un sab ke aamaal ko isi tarah hasrat bana kar pesh karega aur un mein se koi Jahannam se niklne waala nahi hai.

168. Ay insaano! Zameen mein jo kuch bhi halaal-o-tayyab hai usey istemaal karo aur shaitaani iqdamaat ka itteba na karo keh woh tumhaara khula huwa dushman hai.

169. Woh bas tumhe bad-amali aur bad-kaari ka hukm deta hai aur is baat par amaada karta hai ke Khuda ke khilaaf jehaalat ki baate karte raho.

170. Jab un se kaha jaata hai keh jo kuch Khuda ne naazil kiya hai uska itteba karo to kehte hai keh ham uska itteba karege jis par ham ne apne baap-dada ko paya hai. Kya yeh aisa hi karege chahe unke baap-dada be-aql hi rahe ho aur hidaayat yaafta na rahe ho.

171. Jo log kaafir ho gaye hai unke pukaarne waale ki misaal us shakhs ki hai jo jaanwaro ko aawaaz de aur jaanwar pukaar aur aawaaz ke alaawa kuch na soone aur na samjhe. Yeh kuffaar behre, goonge aur andhe hai. inhe aql se saro-kaar nahi hai.

172. Sahebaan-e-imaan jo Ham ne pakeeza rizq ataa kiya hai usey khaawo aur dene waale Khuda ka shukriya adaa karo agar tum uski ibaadat karte ho.

173. Us ne tumhaare upar bas murdaar, khoon, suwwar ka gosht aur jo ghair-e-Khuda ke naam par zibah kiya jaaye us ko haraam qaraar diya hai phir bhi agar koi muztar (laachaar) ho jaaye aur haraam ka talabgaar aur zarurat se zeyada istemaal karne waala na ho to uske liye koi gunah nahi hai. Be-shak Khuda bakhshne waala aur maherbaan hai.

174. Jo log Khuda ki naazil ki huwi kitaab ke ehkaam ko chhupaate hai aur usey thodi qeemat par bechh daaltey hai woh dar-haqeeqat apne pet mein sirf aag bhar rahe hai aur Khuda roz-e-qayamat un se baat bhi na karega aur na unhe pakeeza qaraar dega aur unke liye dard-naak azaab hai.

175. Yahi woh log hai jinho ne gumraahi ko hidaayat ke ewaz aur azaab ko maghferat ke ewaz khareed liya hai aakhri aatish-e-Jahannam (dozakh ki aag) par kis qadr sabr karege.

176. Yeh azaab sirf is liye hai keh Allah ne kitaab ko haq ke saath naazil kiya hai aur us mein ikhtelaaf karne waale haq se bohot dur ho kar jaghda kar rahe hai.

177. Neki yeh nahi hai keh apna rukh mashriq aur maghrib ki taraf kar lo bal-keh neki us shakhs ka hissa hai jo Allah, aakherat, malaayeka, aur kitaab par imaan le aaye aur mohabbat-e-Khuda mein qarabat-daaro, yateemo, miskeeno ghurbat-zada musaafiro, sawaal karne waalo, aur ghulamo ki azaadi ke liye maal de aur namaaz qaayem kare aur zakaat adaa kare aur jo bhi ahed kare usey pura kare aur faqr-o-faaqa mein aur pareshaniyo aur bimaariyo mein aur maidaan-e-jangh ke haalaat mein sabr karne waale ho to yahi log apne daawaa-e-imaan-o-ehsaan mein sachche hai aur yahi sahebaan-e-taqwa aur parhezgaar hai.

178. Imaan waalo! tumhaare upar maqtuleen ke baare mein qisaas likh diya gaya hai azaad ke badle azaad aur ghulam ke badle ghulam aur aurat ke badle aurat. Ab agar kisi ko maqtool (victim) ke waaris ki taraf se maafi mil jaaye to neki ka itteba kare aur ehsaan ke saath uske haq ko adaa kar de. Yeh Parwardigaar ki taraf se tumhaare haq mein takhfeef (kami) aur rehmat hai lekin ab jo shakhs zeyadati karega uske liye dard-naak azaab bhi hai.

179. Sahebaan-e-aql tumhaare liye qisaas mein zindagi hai ke shaayad tum is tarah muttaqi ban jaawo.

180. Tumhare upar yeh bhi likh diya hai keh jab tum mein se kisi ki maut saamne aa jaaye to agar koi maal chhoda hai to apne maa-baap aur qarabat-daaro ke liye wasiyat kar de yeh sahebaan-e-taqwa par ek tarah ka haq hai.

181. Is ke baad wasiyat ko soon kar jo shakhs tabdeel kar dega uska gunah tabdeel karne waale par hoga tum par nahi. Khuda sab ka soone waala aur sab ke haalaat se ba-khabar hai.

182. Phir agar koi shakhs wasiyat karne waale ki taraf se tarf-daari ya na-insaafi ka khauf rakhta ho aur woh warsa (waaras-daaro) mein sulah kara de to us par koi gunah nahi hai. Allah bada bakhshne waala aur maher-baan hai.

183. Sahebaan-e-imaan tumhaare upar roze usi tarah likh diye gaye hai jis tarah tumhaare pehle waalo par likhe gaye thay shaayad tum is tarah muttaqi ban jaawo.

184. Yeh roze sirf chand din ke hai lekin iske baad bhi koi shakhs mareez hai ya safar mein hai to itne hi din dusre zamaane mein rakh lega aur jo log sirf shiddat aur mashaqqat ki bina par roze nahi rakh sakte hai woh ek miskeen ko khaana khila de aur agar apni taraf se zeyada neki kar de to aur behtar hai… lekin roza rakhna baher-haal tumhaare haq mein behtar hai agar tum sahebaan-e-ilm-o-khabar ho.

185. Mahe Ramazaan woh maheena hai jis mein Qur’an naazil kiya gaya hai jo logo ke liye hidaayat hai aur us mein hidaayat aur haq-o-baatil ke imtiyaz ki waazeh nishaaniya maujood hai lehaaza jo shakhs is maheene mein haazir rahe uska farz hai keh roza rakkhe aur jo mareez ya musaafir ho woh utne hi din dusre zamaane mein rakkhe. Khuda tumhaare baare mein aasaani chahta hai zehmat nahi chahta. Aur utne hi din ka hukm is liye hai keh tum adad poore kar do aur Allah taala ki di huwi hidaayat par uski kibriyayi ka iqraar karo aur shaayad tum is tarah uske shukr-guzaar bande ban jaawo.

186. Aur ay Paighambar! Agar mere bande tum se mere baare mein sawaal kare to Mai un se qareeb hoon. Pukaarne waale ki aawaaz soonta hoon jab bhi pukaarta hai lehaaza mujh se talab-e-qabuliat kare aur mujh hi par imaan-o-eatmaad rakkhe keh shaayad is tarah raahe raast par aa jaaye.

187. Tumhare liye mahe ramazaan ki raat mein aurto’n ke paas jaana halaal kar diya gaya hai. Woh tumhaare liye parda-posh hai aur tum unke liye. Khuda ko maaloom hai keh tum apne hi nafs se khayaanat karte thay to us ne tumhaari tauba qabool kar ke tumhe maaf kar diya. Ab tum ba-itminaan mubasherat karo aur jo Khuda ne tumhaare liye muqaddar kiya hai uski aarzoo karo aur us waqt tak khaa-pee sakte ho jab tak fajr ka siyaah dora, safaid dore se numaya na ho jaaye. Iske baad raat ki siyaahi tak roze ko pura karo aur khabar-daar! Masjido mein etekaaf ke mauqe par aurto’n se mubasherat na karna. Yeh sab muqarrara hudood-e-ilaahi hai. Unke qareeb bhi na jaana. Allah is tarah apni aayato ko logo ke liye waazeh taur par bayaan karta hai keh shaayad woh muttaqi aur parhezgaar ban jaaye.

188. Aur khabar-daar! Ek dusre ka maal najaayez tareeqe se na khaana aur na hukkaam ke hawaale kar dena keh rishwat de kar haraam tareeqe se logo ke amwaal ko kha jaawo. Jab-keh tum jaante ho keh yeh tumhaara maal nahi hai.

189. Ay Paighambar yeh log aap se chaand ke baare mein sawaal karte hai to farmadijiye keh yeh logo ke liye aur hajj ke liye waqt maaloom karne ka zariya hai. Aur yeh koi neki nahi hai ke makanaat mein pichwaade (backside) ki taraf se aawo, bal-keh neki unke liye hai jo parhezgaar ho aur makanaat mein darwaazo ki taraf se aaye aur Allah se daro shaayad tum kaam-yaab ho jaawo.

190. Jo log tum se jangh karte hai tum bhi un se raahe Khuda mein jehaad karo aur zeyadati na karo ke Khuda zeyadati karne waalo ko dost nahi rakhta.

191. Aur un mushreqeen ko jahan paao qatl kar do aur jis tarah unho ne tum ko aawara watan kar diya hai tum bhi unhe nikaal baahar kar do. Aur fitna pardaazi to qatl se bhi badtar hai. Aur un se masjidul haraam ke paas us waqt tak jangh na karna jab tak woh tum se jangh na kare. Iske baad jangh chhayd de to tum bhi chup na betho aur jangh karo keh yahi kaafereen ki saza hai.

192. Phir agar jangh se baaz aa jaaye to Khuda bada bakhshne waala maher-baan hai.

193. Aur un se us waqt tak jangh jaari rakkho jab tak saara fitna khatm na ho jaaye aur deen sirf Allah ka na rahe jaaye phir agar woh log baaz aa jaaye to zaalemeen ke alaawa kisi par zeyadati jaayez nahi hai.

194. Shahere haraam ka jawaab Shahere haraam hai aur hurmat ka bhi qisaas hai lehaaza jo tum par zeyadati kare tum bhi waisa hi bartaaw karo jaisi zeyadati us ne ki hai aur Allah se darte raho aur yeh samajh lo keh Khuda parhezgaaro hi ke saath hai.

195. Aur raahe Khuda mein kharch karo aur apne nafs ko halaakat mein na daalo. Nek bartaaw karo ke Khuda nek amal karne waalo ke saath hai.

196 Hajj aur umrah ko Allah ke liye tamaam karo ab agar ghiraf-taar ho jaawo to jo qurbaani mumkin ho woh de do aur us waqt tak sar na mundwaao jab tak qurbaani apni manzil tak na pahonch jaaye. Ab jo tum mein se mareez hai ya uske sar mein koi takleef hai to woh roza ya sadqa ya qurbaani de-de phir jab itminaan ho jaaye to jisne umrah se hajje tamatto ka iraada kiya hai woh mumkina qurbaani de-de aur qurbaani na mil sake to teen roze hajj ke dauraan aur saat waapas ane ke baad rakkhe keh is tarah das poore ho jaaye. Yeh hajje tamatto aur qurbaani un logo ke liye hai jin ke Ahle masjidul haraam ke haazir shumaar nahi hote aur Allah se darte raho aur yeh yaad rakkho ke Khuda ka azaab bohot sakht hai.

197. Hajj chand muqarrara mahino mein hota hai aur jo shakhs bhi is zamaane mein apne upar hajj laazim kar le usey aurto’n se mubasherat gunah aur jaghde ki ijaazat nahi hai aur tum jo bhi khair karoge Khuda usey jaanta hai apne liye zaade raah faraaham karo ke behtareen zaade raah taqwa hai aur ay sahebaan-e-aql! Ham se daro.

198. Tumhare liye koi harj nahi hai keh apne Parwardigaar ke fazl-o-karam ko talaash karo phir jab Arafat se kunch karo to mash-arool haraam ke paas zikre Khuda karo aur is tarah zikr karo jis tarah us ne hidaayat di hai agar-che tum log iske pehle gumraaho mein se thay.

199. Phir tamaam logo ki tarah tum bhi kuch karo aur Allah se isteghfaar karo keh Allah bada bakhshne waala aur maher-baan hai.

200. Phir jab saare manaasik (aamaal) tamaam kar lo to Khuda ko usi tarah yaad rakkho jis tarah apne baap-dada ko yaad karte ho bal-keh us se bhi zeyada ke baaz log aise hai jo kehte hai keh Parwardigaar hamein duniya hi mein neki de-de aur unka aakherat mein koi hissa nahi hai.

201. Aur baaz kehte hai keh Parwardigaar hamein duniya mein bhi neki ataa farma aur aakherat mein bhi aur ham ko azaab-e-Jahannam se mehfooz farma.

202. Yahi woh log hai jin ke liye unki kamaai ka hissa hai aur Khuda bohot jald hisaab karne waala hai.

203. Aur chand mo’ayyan dino mein zikre Khuda karo. Uske baad jo do din ke andar jaldi karega us par bhi koi gunah nahi hai aur jo taakheer karega us par bhi koi gunah nahi hai be-sharte ke parhezgaar raha ho aur Allah se daro aur yeh yaad rakkho ke tum sab usi ki taraf mehshoor kiye jaawoge.

204. Insaano mein aise log bhi hai jin ki baate zindagaani-e-duniya mein bhali (achchi) lagti hai aur woh apne dil ki baato par Khuda ko gawah banaate hai haala keh woh bad-tareen dushman hai.

205. Aur jab aap ke paas se mooh pherte hai to zameen mein fasaad barpa karne ki koshish karte hai aur khetiyo aur naslo ko barbaad karte hai jab-keh Khuda fasaad ko pasand nahi karta hai.

206. Jab un se kaha jaata hai ke taqwa-e-ilaahi ikhtiyaar karo to guroor-e-gunah keh aade aa jaata hai aise logo ke liye Jahannam kaafi hai jo bad-tareen thikaana hai.

207. Aur logo mein woh bhi hai jo apne nafs ko marziye Parwardigaar ke liye bechh daalte hai aur Allah apne bando par bada maher-baan hai.

208. Imaan waalo! Tum sab mukammal tareeqe se Islaam mein daakhil ho jaawo aur shaitaani iqdamaat ka itteba na karo keh woh tumhaara khula huwa dushman hai.

209. Phir agar khuli nishaaniya ke aa jaaane ke baad lagzish paiyda ho jaaye to yaad rakkho ke Khuda sab par ghaalib hai aur saheb-e-hikmat hai.

210. Yeh log is baat ka intezaar kar rahe hai keh abr ke saaye ke peechhe azaab-e-Khuda ya malaayeka aa jaaye aur har amr ka faisla ho jaaye aur saare umoor ki baaz-gasht to Khuda hi ki taraf hai.

211. Zara bani Israeel se poonchiye ke Ham ne inhe kis qadr nemate ataa ki hai aur jo shakhs bhi nemato ke aa jaaane ke baad unhe tabdeel kar dega woh yaad rakkhe ke Khuda ka azaab bohot shadeed hota hai.

212. Asl mein kaafiro ke liye zindagaani-e-duniya aaraasta kar di gayi hai aur woh sahebaan-e-imaan ka mazaaq udaate hai haala keh qayamat ke din muttaqi aur parhezgaar afraad ka darjja un se kahi zeyada baala-tar hoga aur Allah jis ko chahta hai be-hisaab rizq deta hai.

213. (Fitri etebaar se) Saare insaan ek qaum thay. Phir Allah ne bashaarat dene waale aur daraane waale ambiya bheje aur unke saath bar-haq kitaab naazil ki ta-keh logo ke ikhtelaafaat ka faisla kare aur asl ikhtelaaf un hi logo ne kiya jinhe kitaab mil gayi hai aur un par aayaat waazeh ho gayi sirf bagaawat aur ta’adi (naafarmaani aur had se aage jaane) ki bina par…. To Khuda ne imaan waalo ko hidaayat de di aur unho ne ikhtelaafaat mein hukm-e-ilaahi se haq daryaaft kar liya aur woh to jis ko chahta hai serat-e-mustaqeem ki hidaayat de deta hai.

214. Kya tumhaara khayaal hai ke tum aasaani se jannat mein daakhil ho jaawoge jab-keh abhi tumhaare saamne saabiq ummato ki misaal pesh nahi aayi jinhe faqr-o-faaqa aur pareshaniyo ne gher liya aur itne jatke diye gaye ke khud Rasool aur unke saathiyo ne yeh kehna shuru kar diya ke aakhir Khudai imdaad kab aayengi. To aagah ho jaawo ke Khudai imdaad bohot qareeb hai.

215. Paighambar yeh log aap se sawaal karte hai keh raahe Khuda mein kya kharch kare to aap kahe dijiye keh jo bhi kharch karoge woh tumhaare waaledain, qaraabat-daar, aytaam, miskeen aur ghurbat-zada musaafiro ke liye hoga aur jo bhi kaar-e-khair karoge Khuda usey khoob jaanta hai.

216. Tumhare upar jehaad farz kiya gaya hai aur woh tumhe na-gawaar hai aur yeh mumkin hai keh jise tum bura samajh-te ho woh tumhaare haq mein behtar ho aur jise tum dost rakhte ho woh bura ho Khuda sab ko jaanta hai aur tum nahi jaante ho.

217. Paighambar yeh aap se mohtaram mahino ke jehaad ke baare mein sawaal karte hai to aap kahe dijiye keh un mein jangh karna gunah-e-kabeera hai aur raahe Khuda se rokna aur Khuda aur masjidul haraam ki hurmat ka inkaar hai aur Ahle masjidul haraam ka wahan se nikaal dena Khuda ki nighah mein jangh se bhi badtar gunah hai aur fitna to qatl se bhi bada jurm hai… aur yeh kuffaar baraabar tum logo se jangh karte rahege yahan tak keh unke imkaan mein ho to tum ko tumhaare deen se palta de. Aur jo bhi apne deen se palat jaayega aur kufr ki haalat mein mar jaayega uske saare aamaal barbaad ho jaayege aur woh jahannami hoga aur wahi hamesha rahega.

218. Be-shak jo log imaan laaye aur jinho ne hijrat ki aur raahe Khuda mein jehaad kiya woh rehmate ilaahi ki umeed rakhte hai aur Khuda bohot bakhshne waala aur maher-baan hai.

219. Yeh aap se sharaab aur juwe ke baare mein sawaal karte hai to kahe dijiye keh un dono mein bohot bada gunah hai aur bohot se faaide bhi hai lekin unka gunah faaide se kahi zeyada bada hai aur yeh raahe Khuda mein kharch ke baare mein sawaal karte hai keh kya kharch kare to kahe dijiye keh jo bhi zarurat se zeyada ho. Khuda isi tarah apni aayaat ko waazeh kar ke bayaan karta hai keh shaayad tum fikr kar sako.

220. Duniya mein bhi aur aakherat mein bhi… aur yeh log tum se yateemo ke baare mein sawaal karte hai to kahe do keh unke haal ki islaah behtareen baat hai aur agar un se mil-jul kar raho to yeh bhi tumhaare bhai hai aur Allah behtar jaanta hai keh musleh (rectifier) kaun hai aur mufseed (corruptor) kaun hai agar woh chahta to tumhe museebat mein daal deta lekin woh saheb-e-izzat bhi hai aur saheb-e-hikmat bhi hai.

221. khabar-daar! Mushriq aurto’n se us waqt tak nikah na karna jab tak imaan na le aaye keh ek momin kaneez mushriq azaad aurat se behtar hai chahe woh tumhe kitni hi bhali (achchi) maaloom ho aur mushreqeen ko bhi ladkiya na dena jab tak musalmaan na ho jaaye keh musalmaan ghulam azaad mushriq se behtar hai chahe woh tumhe kitna hi achcha kyu’n na maaloom ho. yeh mushreqeen tumhe Jahannam ki daawat dete hai aur Khuda apne hukm se jannat aur maghferat ki daawat deta hai aur apni aayato ko waazeh kar ke bayaan karta hai ke shaayad yeh log samajh sakay.

222. Aur ay Paighambar yeh log tum se ayyaame haiz ke baare mein sawaal karte hai to kahe do keh haiz ek azeeyat aur takleef hai lehaaza us zamaane mein aurto’n se alag raho aur jab tak paak na ho jaaye unke qareeb na jaawo phir jab paak ho jaaye to jis tarah se Khuda ne hukm diya hai us tarah unke paas jaawo. Ba-tehqeeq Khuda tauba karne waalo aur pakeeza rehne waalo ko dost rakhta hai.

223. Tumhari aurte’n tumhaari khetiya hai lehaaza apni kheti mein jahan chaaho daakhil ho jaawo aur apne waaste peshgi aamaal Khuda ki baargah mein bhej do aur us se darte raho… yeh samjho keh tumhe us se mulaqaat karna hai aur sahebaan-e-imaan ko bashaarat de-do.

224. khabar-daar! Khuda ko apni qasmo ka nishana na banaawo ke qasmo ko neki karne taqwa ikhtiyaar karne aur logo ke darmiyaan islaah karne mein maane bana do. Allah sab-kuch soonney aur jaanne waala hai.

225. Khuda tumhaari lagw (faaltu) aur gair-iraadi qasmo ka muakhaza (hisaab kitaab) nahi karta hai lekin jis ko tumhaare dilo ne haasil kiya hai uska zaroor muakhaza (hisaab kitaab) karega. Woh bakhshne waala bhi hai aur bardaasht karne waala bhi.

226. Jo log apni biwiyo se tarke jima ki qasam kha lete hai unhe chaar mahine ki mohlat hai. Uske baad waapas aa gaye to Khuda ghafuroor Raheem hai.

227. Aur talaq ka iraada kare to Khuda soon bhi raha hai aur dekh bhi raha hai.

228. Mutallaqa aurte’n teen haiz tak intezaar karenghi aur unhe haq nahi hai keh jo kuch Khuda ne unke rahem mein paiyda kiya hai uski parda-poshi kare (chupa de) agar unka imaan Allah aur aakherat par hai. Aur phir unke shauhar is muddat mein unhe waapas kar lene ke zeyada haq-daar hai agar islaah chahte hai. Aur aurto’n ke liye waise hi huqooq bhi hai jaisi zimme-daariya hai aur mardo ko un par ek imtiyaz haasil hai aur Khuda saheb-e-izzat-o-hikmat hai.

229. Talaq do martaba di jaayegi. Iske baad ya neki ke saath rok liya jaayega ya husne sulooq ke saath azaad kar diya jaayega aur tumhaare liye jaayez nahi hai keh jo kuch unhe de diya hai us mein se kuch waapas lo magar yeh keh yeh andesha ho ke dono hudood-e-ilaahi ko qaayem na rakh sakayge to jab tumhe yeh khauf paiyda ho jaaye keh woh dono hudood-e-ilaahi ko qaayem na rakh sakayge to dono ke liye azaadi hai us fidye ke baare mein jo aurat mard ko de. Lekin yeh hudood-e-ilaahiya hai un se tajaawuz na karna aur jo hudood-e-ilaahi se tajaawuz karega woh zaalemeen mein shumaar hoga.

230. Phir agar teesri martaba talaq de di to aurat mard ke liye halaal na hogi yahan tak keh dusra shauhar kare phir agar woh talaq de-de to dono ke liye koi harj nahi hai ke aapas mein meyl kar le agar yeh khayaal hai ke hudoode-ilaahi ko qaayem rakh sakayge. Yeh hudood-e-ilaahi hai jinhe Khuda sahebaan-e-ilmo ittila (khabar) ke liye waazeh taur se bayaan kar raha hai.

231. Aur jab tum aurto’n ko talaq do aur woh muddate iddat ke khaatme ke qareeb pohonch jaaye to ya unhe islaah aur husne mubasherat ke saath rok lo ya unhe husne sulooq ke saath azaad kar do aur khabar-daar! nuksaan pohonchaane ki garaz se unhe na rokna ke un par zulm karo ke jo aisa karega woh khud apne nafs par zulm karega aur khabar-daar! Ayaate ilaahi ko mazaaq na banaawo. Khuda ki nemat ko yaad karo. Us ne kitaab-o-hikmat ko tumhaari nasihat ke liye naazil kiya hai aur yaad rakkho keh Woh har shaiy ka jaanne waala hai.

232. Aur jab tum log aurto’n ko talaq do aur unki muddate iddat poori ho jaaye to khabar-daar! unhe shauhar karne se na rokna agar woh shauharo (husband) ke saath nek sulooq par raazi ho jaaye. Is hukm ke zariye Khuda unhe nasihat karta hai jin ka imaan Allah aur roze aakherat par hai aur un ehkaam par amal tumhaare liye baeese tazkia bhi hai aur baeese tahaarat bhi. Allah sab-kuch jaanta hai aur tum nahi jaante ho.

233. Aur maae apni aulaad ko do baras kaamil doodh pilaayengi jo raza’at ko pura karna chahega is darmiyaan saheb-e-aulaad ka farz hai keh maao ki roti aur kapde ka munaasib tareeqe se intezaam kare. Kisi shakhs ko uski wus’at se zeyada takleef nahi di ja sakti. Na maa ko uski aulaad ke zariye takleef dene ka haq hai aur na baap ko uski aulaad ke zariye. Aur waaris ki bhi zimme-daari hai ke woh isi tarah ujrat ka intezaam kare. Phir agar dono ba-hami (aapas mein) raza-mandi aur mashwarey se doodh chhudana chahe to koi harj nahi hai aur agar tum apni aulaad ke liye doodh pilaane waali talaash karna chaaho to is mein bhi koi harj nahi hai ba-sharte keh muta’arrif tareeqe ki ujrat adaa kar do aur Allah se daro aur yeh samjho ke woh tumhaare aamaal ko khoob dekh raha hai.

234. Aur jo log tum mein se biwiya chhod kar mar jaaye unki biwiya chaar mahine das din intezaar karengi jab yeh muddat poori ho jaaye to jo munaasib kaam apne haq mein kare us mein koi harj nahi hai Khuda tumhaare aamaal se khoob ba-khabar hai.

235. Tumhare liye nikah ke paighaam ki pesh-kash ya dil hi dil mein poshida iraade mein koi harj nahi hai. Khuda ko maaloom hai keh tum baad mein un se tazkera karoge lekin fil haal khufia waada bhi na lo sirf koi nek baat kahe do to koi harj nahi hai aur jab tak muqarrara muddat poori na ho jaaye aqde nikah ka iraada na karna yeh yaad rakkho ke Khuda tumhaare dil ki baate khoob jaanta hai lehaaza us se darte raho aur yeh jaan lo keh woh Ghafoor bhi hai aur Haleem-o-burdbaar bhi.

236. Aur tum par koi zimme-daari nahi hai agar tum ne aurto’n ko us waqt talaq de di jab-keh un ko chhuwa bhi nahi hai aur unke liye koi mehr bhi mo’ayyan nahi kiya hai al-batta unhe kuch maal-o-mata de do. maal-daar apni haisiyat ke mutaabiq aur gharib apni haisiyat ke mutabiq. Yeh mata be-qadre munaasib hona zaruri hai keh yeh nek kirdaaro par ek haq hai.

237. Aur agar tum ne un ko chhone se pehle talaq de di aur unke liye mehr mo’ayyan kar chuke thay to mo’ayyan mehr ka nisf dena hoga magar yeh keh woh khud maaf kar de ya unka wali maaf kar de aur maaf kar dena taqwa se zeyada qareeb-tar hai aur aapas mein buzurgi ko faraamosh na karo. Khuda tumhaare aamaal ko khoob dekh raha hai.

238. Apni tamaam namaazo aur bil-khusoos namaaze wusta ki muhaafezat aur pa-bandi karo aur Allah ki baargah mein khushoo-o-khuzoo ke saath khade ho jaawo.

239. Phir agar khauf ki haalat ho to paidal, sawaar jis tarah mumkin ho namaaz adaa karo aur jab itminaan ho jaaye to is tarah zikre Khuda karo jis tarah us ne tumhaari la-ilmi mein tumhe bataaya hai.

240. Aur jo log muddate hayaat poori kar rahe ho aur azwaaj ko chhod kar ja rahe ho unhe chaahiye ke apni azwaaj ke liye ek saal ka kharch aur ghar se na nikaalne ki wasiyat kar ke jaaye phir agar woh khud se nikal jaaye to tumhaare liye koi harj nahi hai woh apne baare mein jo bhi munaasib kaam anjaam de Khuda saheb-e-izzat aur saheb-e-hikmat bhi hai.

241. Aur mutallaqa aurto’n ko dastoor ke mutaabiq kuch kharcha dena, yeh muttaqi logo ki zimme-daari hai.

242. Isi tarah Parwardigaar apni aayaat ko bayaan karta hai ke shaayad tumhe aql aa jaaye.

243. Kya tum ne un logo ko nahi dekha jo hazaaro ki tadaad mein apne gharo se nikal pade maut ke khauf se aur Khuda ne unhe maut ka hukm de diya aur phir zinda kar diya ke Khuda logo par bohot fazl karne waala hai lekin aksar log shukriya adaa nahi karte hai.

244. Aur raahe Khuda mein jehaad karo aur yaad rakkho ke Khuda soonne waala bhi hai aur jaanne waala bhi hai.

245. Kaun hai jo Khuda ko karze hasana de aur phir Khuda usey kayee-guna (multiple) kar ke waapas kar de Khuda kam bhi kar sakta hai aur zeyada bhi aur tum sab usi ki baargah mein paltaaye jaawoge.

246. Kya tum ne Moosa alayhis salaam ke baad bani Israeel ki is jamaat ko nahi dekha jisne apne nabi se kaha ke hamare waaste ek badshah muqarrar kijiye ta-keh ham raahe Khuda mein jehaad kare. Nabi ne farmaya keh andesha yeh hai keh tum par jehaad waajib ho jaaye to tum jehaad na karo. Un logo ne kaha keh ham kyu’n kar jehaad na karege jab-keh hamein hamare gharo aur baal bachcho se alag nikaal baahar kar diya gaya hai. Iske baad jab jehaad waajib kar diya gaya to thode se afraad ke alaawa sab munharif ho (haq se palat) gaye aur Allah zaalemeen ko khoob jaanta hai.

247. Unke paighambar alayhis salaam ne kaha keh Allah ne tumhaare liye Taaloot ko haakim muqarrar kiya hai. Un logo ne kaha ke yeh kis tarah hukumat karege unke paas to maal ki farawaani nahi hai un se zeyada to ham hi haqdaare hukumat hai. Nabi ne jawaab diya keh unhe Allah ne tumhaare liye muntakhab kiya hai aur ilm-o-jism mein wus’at ataa farmaayee hai aur Allah jise chahta hai apna mulk de deta hai keh woh saheb-e-wus’at bhi hai aur saheb-e-ilm bhi.

248. Aur unke paighambar alayhis salaam ne yeh bhi kaha keh unki hukumat ki nishaani yeh hai keh tumhaare paas woh taboot le aayege jis mein Parwardigaar ki taraf se saamaane sukoon aur Aale Moosa alayhis salaam aur Aale Haaroon alayhis salaam ka chhoda huwa tarka bhi hai. Us taboot ko malaayeka uthaaye huwe hoge aur us mein tumhaare liye qudrate Parwardigaar ki nishaani bhi hai agar tum saheb-e-imaan ho.

249. Is ke baad jab Taaloot alayhis salaam lashkar le kar chale to unho ne kaha ke ab Khuda ek naher ke zariye tumhaara imtehaan lene waala hai jo us mein se pi lega woh mujh se na hoga aur jo na chakhega woh mujh se hoga magar yeh ke ek chulloo paani le le. Nateeja yeh huwa keh sab ne paani pi liya siwaaye chand afraad ke. Phir jab woh sahebaan-e-imaan ko le kar aaghe badhe, logo ne kaha keh aaj to Jaalut aur uske lashkaro ke muqaable ki himmat nahi hai aur ek jamaat ne jise Khuda se mulaqaat karne ka khayaal tha, kaha ke aksar chhote chhote giroh badi badi jama’ato par hukm-e-Khuda se ghaalib aa jaate hai aur Allah sabr karne waalo ke saath hai.

250. Aur yeh log jab Jaalut aur uske lashkaro ke muqaable ke liye nikle to unho ne kaha ke Khudaaya hamein be panah sabr ataa farma hamare qadmo ko sabaat (solidity) de aur hamein kaafiro ke muqaable mein nusrat ataa farma.

251. Nateeja yeh huwa keh un logo ne Jaalut ke lashkar ko Khuda ke hukm se shikast de di aur Dawood alayhis salaam ne Jaalut ko qatl kar diya aur Allah ne unhe mulk aur hikmat ataa kar di aur apne ilm se jis qadar chaaha de diya aur agar isi tarah Khuda baaz ko baaz se na rokta rehta to saari zameen mein fasaad phail jaata lekin Khuda aalameen par bada fazl karne waala hai.

252. Yeh aayaat-e-ilaahi hai jinko ham waakeyaat ke saath aap ko padh kar soonaate hai aur aap yaqeenan mursaleen mein se hai.

253. Yeh sab Rasool alayhemus salaam woh hai jinhe ham ne baaz ko baaz par fazeelat di hai. Un mein se baaz woh hai jin se Khuda ne kalaam kiya hai aur baaz ke darjaat buland kiye hai aur Ham ne Isa alayhis salaam bin Maryam ko khuli huwi nishaaniya di hai aur Roohul quds ke zariye unki ta’eed ki hai. Agar Khuda chahta to un Rasoolo ke baad waale un waazeh moajezaat ke aa jaane ke baad aapas mein jaghda na karte lekin un logo ne (khuda ke jabr na karne ki bina par) ikhtelaaf kiya hai. Baaz imaan laaye aur baaz kaafir ho gaye aur agar Khuda tai kar leta to yeh jaghda na kar sakte lekin Khuda jo chahta hai wohi karta hai.

254. Ay imaan waalo jo tumhe rizq diya gaya hai us mein se raahe Khuda mein kharch karo qabl uske keh woh din aa jaaye jis din na tijaarat hogi na dosti kaam aayengi aur na sifarish. Aur kaafereen hi asl mein zaalemeen hai.

255. Allah jiske alaawa koi Khuda nahi hai zinda bhi hai aur Usi se kul qaayenaat qaayem hai Usey na neend aati hai na ongh aasmaano aur zameen mein jo kuch bhi hai sab Usi ka hai. Kaun hai jo Uski baargah mein Uski ijaazat ke bagair sifarish kar sake. woh jo kuch unke saamne hai aur jo pas-e-pusht hai sab ko jaanta hai aur yeh Uske ilm ka ek hisse ka bhi ehaata (cover) nahi kar sakte magar Woh jis qadr chahe. Uski khursiye ilm-o-iqtedaar zameen-o-aasmaan se wasee-tar hai aur Usey unke tahaffuz mein koi takleef bhi nahi hoti woh aali martaba bhi hai aur saheb-e-azmat bhi.

256. Deen mein kisi tarah ka jabr nahi hai. Hidaayat gumraahi se alag aur waazeh ho chuki hai. Ab jo shakhs bhi taaghoot ka inkaar kar ke Allah par imaan le aaye woh uski mazboot rassi se tamassuk (mutawassil) ho gaya hai jiske totne ka imkaan nahi hai aur Khuda samee bhi hai aur Aleem bhi hai.

257. Allah sahebaan-e-imaan ka wali hai woh unhe taareekiyo se nikaal kar roshni mein le aata hai aur kuffaar ke wali taaghoot hai jo unhe roshni se nikaal kar andhero mein le jaate hai yahi log jahannami hai aur wahan hamesha rehne waale hai.

258. Kya tum ne uske haal par nazar nahi ki jisne Ibrahim alayhis salaam se Parwardigaar ke baare mein bahes (arguement) ki sirf is baat par ke Khuda ne usey mulk de diya tha jab ibrahim alayhis salaam ne yeh kaha ke mera Khuda jilaata bhi hai aur maarta bhi hai to us ne kaha ke yeh kaam mai bhi kar sakta hoon to Ibrahim alayhis salaam ne kaha ke mera Khuda mashriq se aftaab nikaalta hai tu maghrib se nikaal de to kaafir hairaan rahe gaye aur Allah zaalim qaum ki hidaayat nahi karta hai.

259. Ya us bande ki misaal jiska guzar ek (basti) se huwa jiske saare arsh-o-farsh gir chuke thay to us bande ne kaha ke Khuda un sab ko maut ke baad kis tarah zinda karega to Khuda ne us bande ko sau saal ke liye maut de di aur phir zinda kiya aur poocha ke kitni der pade rahe to us ne kaha ke ek din ya kuch kam. Farmaya nahi, Sau saal. Jara apne khaane aur peene ko to dekho keh kharaab tak nahi huwa aur apne gadhe (donkey) par nighah karo (ke sad-gal gaya hai) aur Ham isi tarah tumhe logo ke liye ek nishaani banaana chahte hai phir un haddiyo ko dekho keh Ham kis tarah jod kar un par gosht chadaate hai. Phir jab un par yeh baat waazeh ho gayi to be-saakhta aawaaz di keh mujhe maaloom hai keh Khuda har shaiy par qaadir hai.

260. Aur us mauqe ko yaad karo jab Ibrahim alayhis salaam ne ilteja ki keh Parwardigaar mujhe yeh dikha de keh Tu murdo ko kis tarah zinda karta hai. Irshaad huwa kya tumhaara imaan nahi hai. Arz ki, imaan to hai lekin itminaan chahta hoon. Irshaad huwa ke chaar tayr (parinda) pakad lo aur unhe apne se maanoos banaawo phir tukde-tukde kar ke har pahaad par ek hissa rakh do aur phir aawaaz do sab daudte huwe aa jaayege aur yaad rakkho ke Khuda saheb-e-izzat bhi hai aur saheb-e-hikmat bhi hai.

261. Jo log raahe Khuda mein apne amwaal kharch karte hai unke amal ki misaal us daane ki hai jis se saat (7) baaliya paiyda ho aur phir har baali mein sau-sau daane ho aur Khuda jiske liye chahta hai izaafah bhi kar deta hai keh Woh saheb-e-wus’at bhi hai aur Aleem-o-dana bhi.

262. Jo log raahe Khuda mein apne amwaal kharch karte hai aur uske baad ehsaan nahi jataate aur azeeyat bhi nahi dete unke liye Parwardigaar ke yahan ajr bhi hai aur na koi khauf hai na huzn (gham).

263. Nek kalaam aur maghferat us sadqe se behtar hai jiske peechhe dil dukhaane ka silsila bhi ho. Khuda sab se be-neyaaz aur bada burdbaar hai.

264. Imaan waalo apne sadaqaat ko minnat guzaari aur azeeyat se barbaad na karo us shakhs ki tarah jo apne maal ko duniya dikhaane ke liye sarf karta hai aur uska imaan na Khuda par hai aur na aakherat par, uski misaal us saaf chattaan ki hai jis par gard jam gayi ho keh tez baarish ke aate hi bilkul saaf ho jaaye yeh log apni kamaai par bhi ikhtiyaar nahi rakhte aur Allah kaafiro ki hidaayat bhi nahi karta.

265. Aur jo log apne amwaal ko raza-e-Khuda ki talab aur apne nafs ke istehkaam ki garaz se kharch karte hai unke maal ki misaal us baagh ki hai jo kisi bulandi par ho aur tez baarish aakar uski fasal dugna bana de aur agar tez baarish na aaye to maamuli baarish hi kaafi ho jaaye aur Allah tumhaare aamaal ki niyyato se khoob ba-khabar hai.

266. Kya tum mein se koi yeh pasand karta hai keh uske paas khajoor aur angoor ke baagh ho. Unke neeche nehre jaari ho un mein har tarah ke phal ho aur aadmi budha ho jaaye. Uske kamzor bachche ho aur phir achaanak tez garam hawa jis mein aag bhari ho chal jaaye aur sab jal kar khaak ho jaaye. Khuda is tarah apni aayaat ko waazeh kar ke bayaan karta hai keh shaayad tum fikr kar sako.

267. Ay imaan waalo apni pakeeza kamaai aur jo kuch Ham ne zameen se tumhaare liye paiyda kiya hai sab mein se raahe Khuda mein kharch karo aur khabar-daar! Infaaq ke iraade se kharaab maal ko haath bhi na lagaana keh agar yeh maal tum ko diya jaaye to aankh bandh kiye bagair chhuonge bhi nahi yaad rakkho ke Khuda sab se be-neyaaz hai aur saza-waar hamd-o-sana bhi hai.

268. Shaitaan tum se faqeeri ka waada karta hai aur tumhe buraaiyo ka hukm deta hai aur Khuda maghferat aur fazl-o-ehsaan ka waada karta hai. Khuda saheb-e-wus’at bhi hai aur Aleem-o-dana bhi.

269. Woh jis ko bhi chahta hai hikmat ataa kar deta hai aur jise hikmat ataa kar di jaaye usey goya khair-e-kaseer ataa kar diya gaya aur is baat ko sahebaan-e-aql ke alaawa koi nahi samjhta hai.

270. Aur tum jo kuch bhi raahe Khuda mein kharch karoge ya nazr karoge to Khuda us se ba-khabar hai al-batta zaalemeen ka koi madad-gaar nahi hai.

271. Agar tum sadqe ko alal-elaan donge to yeh bhi theek hai aur agar chhipa kar foqara ke hawaale kar donge to yeh bhi bohot behtar hai aur iske zariye tumhaare bohot se gunah maaf ho jaayege aur Khuda tumhaare aamaal se khoob ba-khabar hai.

272. Ay Paighambar! Unki hidaayat pa jaane ki zimme-daari aap par nahi hai bal-keh Khuda jis ko chahta hai hidaayat de deta hai aur logo! Jo maal bhi tum raahe Khuda mein kharch karoge woh dar-asal apne hi liye hoga aur tum to sirf khushnoodi-e-Khuda ke liye kharch karte ho aur jo kuch bhi kharch karoge woh pura pura tumhaari taraf waapas aayega aur tum par kisi tarah ka zulm na hoga.

273. Yeh sadqa un foqara ke liye hai jo raahe Khuda mein ghiraf-taar ho gaye hai aur kisi taraf jaane ke qaabil bhi nahi hai na-waaqif afraad unhe unki haya-o-iffat ki bina par maal-daar samajh-te hai haala keh tum aasaar se unki ghurbat ka andaaza kar sakte ho agar-che logo se ceemat kar sawaal nahi karte hai aur tum log jo kuch bhi infaaq karoge Khuda usey khoob jaanta hai.

274. Jo log apne amwaal ko raahe Khuda mein raat mein, din mein khaamoshi se aur alal-elaan kharch karte hai unke liye pesh-e-Parwardigaar ajr bhi hai aur unhe na koi khauf hoga aur na huzn (gham).

275. Jo log sood (byaaj) khaate hai woh roz-e-qayamat us shakhs ki tarah uthaynge jise shaitaan ne chhu kar makhbootul hawaas (paagal) bana diya ho is liye keh unho ne yeh kahe diya hai keh tijaarat bhi sood jaisi hai jab-keh Khuda ne tijaarat ko halaal qaraar diya hai aur sood ko haraam. Ab jiske paas Khuda ki taraf se nasihat aa gayi aur us ne sood ko tark kar diya to guzishta kaar-o-baar ka maamla Khuda ke hawaale hai aur jo iske baad bhi sood le to woh log sab jahannami hai aur wahi hamesha rehne waale hai.

276. Khuda sood ko barbaad kar deta hai aur sadaqaat mein izaafah kar deta hai aur Khuda kisi bhi na-shukre gunahgaar ko dost nahi rakhta.

277. Jo log imaan le aaye aur unho ne nek amal kiye namaaz qaayem ki. Zakaat adaa ki unke liye Parwardigaar ke yahan ajr hai aur unke liye kisi tarah ka khauf ya huzn (gham) nahi hai.

278. Imaan waalo Allah se daro aur jo sood baaqi rahe gaya hai usey chhod do agar tum sahebaan-e-imaan ho.

279. Agar tum ne aisa na kiya to Khuda-o-Rasool se jangh karne ke liye tayyar ho jaawo aur agar tauba kar lo to asl maal tumhaara hi hai. Na tum zulm karoge na tum par zulm kiya jaayega.

280. Aur agar tumhaara maqrooz tang-dast hai to usey wus’ate haal tak mohlat di jaayega aur agar tum maaf kar donge to tumhaare haq mein zeyada behtar hai be-sharte keh tum usey samajh sako.

281. Us din se daro jab tum sab palta kar Allah ki baargah mein le jaaye jaawoge iske baad har nafs ko uske kiye ka pura-pura badla milega aur kisi par koi zulm nahi kiya jaayega.

282. Imaan waalo jab bhi aapas mein ek muqarrara muddat ke liye karz ka len-den karo to usey likh lo aur tumhaare darmiyaan koi bhi kaatib likhe lekin insaaf ke saath likhe aur kaatib ko na chaahiye ke Khuda ki taaleem ke mutaabiq likhne se inkaar kare. Usey likh dena chaahiye aur jiske zimme karz hai us ko chaahiye keh woh imla (dictation) kare aur us Khuda se darta rahe jo uska paalne waala hai aur kisi tarah ki kami na kare. Ab agar jiske zimme karz hai woh naadaan kamzor ya mazmoon (article) bataane ke qaabil nahi hai to uska wali mazmoon (article) tayyar kare.… aur apne mardo mein se do (2) ko gawah banaawo aur do mard na ho to ek (1) mard aur do (2) aurte’n ta-keh ek behkne lagey to dusri yaad dila de aur gawaho ko chaahiye ke gawahi ke liye bulaaye jaaye to inkaar na kare aur khabar-daar! Likha-padhi se na-gwaari (indolence) ka izhaar na karna, chahe karz chhota ho ya bada muddat mo’ayyan honi chaahiye. Yahi Parwardigaar ke nazdeek adaalat ke mutaabiq aur gawahi ke liye zeyada mustahkam (mazboot) tareeqa hai aur us amr se qareeb-tar hai ke aapas mein shak-o-shubha na paiyda ho… haa’n agar tijaarat naqd (cash) hai jis se tum log aapas mein amwaal ki ulat-pher karte ho to na likhne mein koi harj bhi nahi hai aur agar tijaarat mein bhi gawah banaawo to kaatib ya gawah ko haq nahi ke apne tarze (ravish) amal se logo ko nuksaan pohonchaaye aur na logo ko yeh haq hai aur agar tum ne aisa kiya to yeh ita’ate Khuda se na-farmaani hai.

283. Aur agar tum safar mein ho aur koi kaatib nahi mil raha hai to koi rehaan (amaanat) rakh do aur ek ko dusre par etebaar ho to jis par etebaar hai us ko chaahiye keh amaanat ko waapas kar de aur Khuda se darta rahe… aur khabar-daar! Gawahi ko chhupana nahi keh jo aisa karega uska dil gunah-gaar hoga aur Allah tumhaare aamaal se khoob ba-khabar hai.

284. Allah hi ke liye zameen-o-aasmaan ki kul qaayenaat hai tum apne dil ki baato ka izhaar karo ya un par parda daalo woh sab ka muhaasba karega Woh jis ko chahega bakhsh dega aur jis par chahega azaab karega woh har shaiy par qudrat-o-ikhtiyaar rakhne waala hai.

285. Rasool un tamaam baato par imaan rakhta hai jo uski taraf naazil ki gayi hai aur momenin bhi, sab Allah aur malaayeka aur mursaleen par imaan rakhte hai un ka kehna hai ke ham Rasoolo ke darmiyaan tafreeq (distinction) nahi karte. Ham ne paighaam-e-ilaahi ko soona aur uski ita’at ki Parwardigaar ab Teri maghferat dar-kaar hai aur Teri hi taraf palat kar aana hai.

286. Allah kisi nafs ko uski wus’at se zeyada takleef nahi deta. Har nafs ke liye uski haasil ki huwi nekiyo ka faaida bhi hai aur uski kamaai huwi buraaiyo ka mazlamah bhi…. Parwardigaar! Ham jo kuch bhool jaaye ya ham se galti ho jaaye uska ham se muakheza (hisaab kitaab) na karna. Khudaaya! Ham par waisa bojh na daalna jaisa pehle waali ummato par dala gaya hai Parwardigaar! Ham par woh baar na daalna jiski ham mein taaqat na ho. Hamein maaf kar dena hamein bakhsh dena ham par rahem karna tu hamara moula aur maalik hai ab kaafiro ke muqaable mein hamari madad farma.

2 | BAQARAH | 286

In the name of Allah, the Beneficent, the Merciful.

1. Alif Lam Mim.

2. This Book, there is no doubt in it, is a guide to those who guard (against evil).

3. Those who believe in the unseen and keep up prayer and spend out of what We have given them.

4. And who believe in that which has been revealed to you and that which was revealed before you and they are sure of the hereafter.

5. These are on a right course from their Lord and these it is that shall be successful.

6. Surely those who disbelieve, it being alike to them whether you warn them, or do not warn them, will not believe.

7. Allah has set a seal upon their hearts and upon their hearing and there is a covering over their eyes, and there is a great punishment for them.

8. And there are some people who say: We believe in Allah and the last day; and they are not at all believers.

9. They desire to deceive Allah and those who believe, and they deceive only themselves and they do not perceive.

10. There is a disease in their hearts, so Allah added to their disease and they shall have a painful chastisement because they lied.

11. And when it is said to them, Do not make mischief in the land, they say: We are but peace-makers.

12. Now surely they themselves are the mischief makers, but they do not perceive.

13. And when it is said to them: Believe as the people believe, they say: Shall we believe as the fools believe? Now surely they themselves are the fools, but they do not know.

14. And when they meet those who believe, they say: We believe; and when they are alone with their evil ones, they say: Surely we are with you, we were only mocking.

15. Allah shall pay them back their mockery, and He leaves them alone in their inordinacy, blindly wandering on.

16. These are they who buy error for the right direction, so their bargain shall bring no gain, nor are they the followers of the right direction.

17. Their parable is like the parable of one who kindled a fire but when it had illumined all around him, Allah took away their light, and left them in utter darkness— they do not see.

18. Deaf, dumb (and) blind, so they will not turn back.

19. Or like abundant rain from the cloud in which is utter darkness and thunder and lightning; they put their fingers into their ears because of the thunder peal, for fear of death, and Allah encompasses the unbelievers.

20. The lightning almost takes away their sight; whenever it shines on them they walk in it, and when it becomes dark to them they stand still; and if Allah had pleased He would certainly have taken away their hearing and their sight; surely Allah has power over all things.

21. O men! serve your Lord Who created you and those before you so that you may guard (against evil).

22. Who made the earth a resting place for you and the heaven a canopy and (Who) sends down rain from the cloud, then brings forth with it subsistence for you of the fruits; therefore do not set up rivals to Allah while you know.

23. And if you are in doubt as to that which We have revealed to Our servant, then produce a chapter like it and call on your witnesses besides Allah if you are truthful.

24. But if you do (it) not and never shall you do (it), then be on your guard against the fire of which men and stones are the fuel; it is prepared for the unbelievers.

25. And convey good news to those who believe and do good deeds, that they shall have gardens in which rivers flow; when-
ever they shall be given a portion of the fruit thereof, they shall say: This is what was given to us before; and they shall be given the like of it, and they shall have pure mates in them, and in
them, they shall abide.

26. Surely Allah is not ashamed to set forth any parable—
(that of) a lowest or any thing above that; then as for those who
believe, they know that it is the truth from their Lord, and as for those who disbelieve, they say: What is it that Allah means by
this parable: He causes many to err by it and many He leads
aright by it! but He does not cause to err by it (any) except the transgressors,

27. Who break the covenant of Allah after its confirmation
and cut asunder what Allah has ordered to be joined, and make mischief in the land; these it is that are the losers.

28. How do you deny Allah and you were dead and He gave you life? Again He will cause you to die and again bring you to life, then you shall be brought back to Him.

29. He it is Who created for you all that is in the earth, and He directed Himself to the heaven, so He made them complete
seven heavens, and He knows all things.

30. And when your Lord said to the angels, I am going to
place in the earth a vicegerent, they said: What! wilt Thou place in it such as shall make mischief in it and shed blood, and we cele-brate Thy praise and extol Thy holiness? He said: Surely I know what you do not know.

31. And He taught Adam all the names, then presented them
to the angels; then He said: Tell me the names of those if you are right.

32. They said: Glory be to Thee! we have no knowledge but
that which Thou hast taught us; surely Thou art the Knowing,
the Wise.

33. He said: O Adam! inform them of their names. Then
when he had informed them of their names, He said: Did I not
say to you that I surely know what is secret in the heavens and the earth and (that) I know what you manifest and what you
hide?

34. And when We said to the angels: Make obeisance to
Adam they did obeisance, but Satan (did it not). He refused and
he was proud, and he was one of the unbelievers.

35. And We said: O Adam! Dwell you and your wife in the
garden and eat from it a plenteous (food) wherever you wish and do not approach this tree, for then you will be of the unjust.

36. But the Shaitan made them both fall from it, and caused them to depart from that (state) in which they were; and We said: Get forth, some of you being the enemies of others, and there is for you in the earth an abode and a provision for a time.

37. Then Adam received (some) words from his Lord, so He turned to him mercifully; surely He is Oft-returning (to mercy), the Merciful.

38. We said: Go forth from this (state) all; so surely there will come to you a guidance from Me, then whoever follows My guidance, no fear shall come upon them, nor shall they grieve.

39. And (as to) those who disbelieve in and reject My communications, they are the inmates of the fire, in it they shall abide.

40. O children of Israel! call to mind My favor which I bestowed on you and be faithful to (your) covenant with Me, I will fulfill (My) covenant with you; and of Me, Me alone, should you be afraid.

41. And believe in what I have revealed, verifying that which is with you, and be not the first to deny it, neither take a mean price in exchange for My communications; and Me, Me alone should you fear.

42. And do not mix up the truth with the falsehood, nor hide the truth while you know (it).

43. And keep up prayer and pay the poor-rate and bow down with those who bow down.

44. What! do you enjoin men to be good and neglect your own souls while you read the Book; have you then no sense?

45. And seek assistance through patience and prayer, and most surely it is a hard thing except for the humble ones,

46. Who know that they shall meet their Lord and that they shall return to Him.

47. O children of Israel! call to mind My favor which I bestowed on you and that I made you excel the nations.

48. And be on your guard against a day when one soul shall not avail another in the least, neither shall intercession on its behalf be accepted, nor shall any compensation be taken from it, nor shall they be helped.

49. And when We delivered you from Firon’s people, who subjected you to severe torment, killing your sons and sparing your women, and in this there was a great trial from your Lord.

50. And when We parted the sea for you, so We saved you and drowned the followers of Firon and you watched by.

51. And when We appointed a time of forty nights with Musa, then you took the calf (for a god) after him and you were unjust.

52. Then We pardoned you after that so that you might give thanks.

53. And when We gave Musa the Book and the distinction that you might walk aright.

54. And when Musa said to his people: O my people! you have surely been unjust to yourselves by taking the calf (for a god), therefore turn to your Creator (penitently), so kill your people, that is best for you with your Creator: so He turned to you (mercifully), for surely He is the Oft-returning (to mercy), the Merciful.

55. And when you said: O Musa! we will not believe in you until we see Allah manifestly, so the punishment overtook you while you looked on.

56. Then We raised you up after your death that you may give thanks.

57. And We made the clouds to give shade over you and We sent to you manna and quails: Eat of the good things that We have given you; and they did not do Us any harm, but they made their own souls suffer the loss.

58. And when We said: Enter this city, then eat from it a plenteous (food) wherever you wish, and enter the gate making obeisance, and say, forgiveness. We will forgive you your wrongs and give more to those who do good (to others).

59. But those who were unjust changed it for a saying other than that which had been spoken to them, so We sent upon those who were unjust a pestilence from heaven, because they transgressed.

60. And when Musa prayed for drink for his people, We said: Strike the rock with your staff. So there gushed from it twelve springs; each tribe knew its drinking place: Eat and drink of the provisions of Allah and do not act corruptly in the land, making mischief.

61. And when you said: O Musa! we cannot bear with one food, therefore pray Lord on our behalf to bring forth for us out of what the earth grows, of its herbs and its cucumbers and its garlic and its lentils and its onions. He said: Will you exchange that which is better for that which is worse? Enter a city, so you will have what you ask for. And abasement and humiliation were brought down upon them, and they became deserving of Allah’s wrath; this was so because they disbelieved in the communications of Allah and killed the prophets unjustly; this was so because they disobeyed and exceeded the limits.

62. Surely those who believe, and those who are Jews, and the Christians, and the Sabians, whoever believes in Allah and the Last day and does good, they shall have their reward from their Lord, and there is no fear for them, nor shall they grieve.

63. And when We took a promise from you and lifted the mountain over you: Take hold of the law (Tavrat) We have given you with firmness and bear in mind what is in it, so that you may guard (against evil).

64. Then you turned back after that; so were it not for the grace of Allah and His mercy on you, you would certainly have been among the losers.

65. And certainly you have known those among you who exceeded the limits of the Sabbath, so We said to them: Be (as) apes, despised and hated.

66. So We made them an example to those who witnessed it and those who came after it, and an admonition to those who guard (against evil).

67. And when Musa said to his people: Surely Allah commands you that you should sacrifice a cow; they said: Do you ridicule us? He said: I seek the protection of Allah from being one of the ignorant.

68. They said: Call on your Lord for our sake to make it plain to us what she is. Musa said: He says, Surely she is a cow neither advanced in age nor too young, of middle age between that (and this); do therefore what you are commanded.

69. They said: Call on your Lord for our sake to make it plain to us what her color is. Musa said: He says, Surely she is a yellow cow; her color is intensely yellow, giving delight to the beholders.

70. They said: Call on your Lord for our sake to make it plain to us what she is, for surely to us the cows are all alike, and if Allah please we shall surely be guided aright.

71. Musa said: He says, Surely she is a cow not made submissive that she should plough the land, nor does she irrigate the tilth; sound, without a blemish in her. They said: Now you have brought the truth; so they sacrificed her, though they had not the mind to do (it).

72. And when you killed a man, then you disagreed with respect to that, and Allah was to bring forth that which you were going to hide.

73. So We said: Strike the (dead body) with part of the (Sacrificed cow), thus Allah brings the dead to life, and He shows you His signs so that you may understand.

74. Then your hearts hardened after that, so that they were like rocks, rather worse in hardness; and surely there are some rocks from which streams burst forth, and surely there are some of them which split asunder so water issues out of them, and surely there are some of them which fall down for fear of Allah, and Allah is not at all heedless of what you do.

75. Do you then hope that they would believe in you, and a party from among them indeed used to hear the Word of Allah, then altered it after they had understood it, and they know (this).

76. And when they meet those who believe they say: We believe, and when they are alone one with another they say: Do you talk to them of what Allah has disclosed to you that they may contend with you by this before your Lord? Do you not then understand?

77. Do they not know that Allah knows what they keep secret and what they make known?

78. And there are among them illiterates who know not the Book but only lies, and they do but conjecture.

79. Woe, then, to those who write the book with their hands and then say: This is from Allah, so that they may take for it a small price; therefore woe to them for what their hands have written and woe to them for what they earn.

80. And they say: Fire shall not touch us but for a few days. Say: Have you received a promise from Allah, then Allah will not fail to perform His promise, or do you speak against Allah what you do not know?

81. Yea! whoever earns evil and his sins beset him on every side, these are the inmates of the fire; in it they shall abide.

82. And (as for) those who believe and do good deeds, these are the dwellers of the garden; in it they shall abide.

83. And when We made a covenant with the children of Israel: You shall not serve any but Allah and (you shall do) good to (your) parents, and to the near of kin and to the orphans and the needy, and you shall speak to men good words and keep up prayer and pay the poor-rate. Then you turned back except a few of you and (now too) you turn aside.

84. And when We made a covenant with you: You shall not shed your blood and you shall not turn your people out of your cities; then you gave a promise while you witnessed.

85. Yet you it is who slay your people and turn a party from among you out of their homes, backing each other up against them unlawfully and exceeding the limits; and if they should come to you, as captives you would ransom them— while their very turning out was unlawful for you. Do you then believe in a part of the Book and disbelieve in the other? What then is the reward of such among you as do this but disgrace in the life of this world, and on the day of resurrection they shall be sent back to the most grievous chastisement, and Allah is not at all heedless of what you do.

86. These are they who buy the life of this world for the hereafter, so their chastisement shall not be lightened nor shall they be helped.

87. And most certainly We gave Musa the Book and We sent apostles after him one after another; and We gave Isa, the son of Marium, clear arguments and strengthened him with the holy spirit, What! whenever then an apostle came to you with that which your souls did not desire, you were insolent so you called some liars and some you slew.

88. And they say: Our hearts are covered. Nay, Allah has cursed them on account of their unbelief; so little it is that they believe.

89. And when there came to them a Book from Allah verifying that which they have, and aforetime they used to pray for victory against those who disbelieve, but when there came to them (Prophet) that which they did not recognize, they disbelieved in him; so Allah’s curse is on the unbelievers.

90. Evil is that for which they have sold their souls— that they should deny what Allah has revealed, out of envy that Allah should send down of His grace on whomsoever of His servants He pleases; so they have made themselves deserving of wrath upon wrath, and there is a disgraceful punishment for the unbelievers.

91. And when it is said to them, Believe in what Allah has revealed, they say: We believe in that which was revealed to us; and they deny what is besides that, while it is the truth verifying that which they have. Say: Why then did you kill Allah’s Prophets before if you were indeed believers?

92. And most certainly Musa came to you with clear arguments, then you took the calf (for a god) in his absence and you were unjust.

93. And when We made a covenant with you and raised the mountain over you: Take hold of what We have given you with firmness and be obedient. They said: We hear and disobey. And they were made to imbibe (the love of) the calf into their hearts on account of their unbelief. Say: Evil is that which your belief bids you if you are believers.

94. Say: If the future abode with Allah is specially for you to the exclusion of the people, then invoke death if you are truthful.

95. And they will never invoke it on account of what their hands have sent before, and Allah knows the unjust.

96. And you will most certainly find them the greediest of men for life (greedier) than even those who are polytheists; every one of them loves that he should be granted a life of a thousand years, and his being granted a long life will in no way remove him further off from the chastisement, and Allah sees what they do.

97. Say: Whoever is the enemy of Jibreel— for surely he revealed it to your heart by Allah’s command, verifying that which is before it and guidance and good news for the believers.

98. Whoever is the enemy of Allah and His angels and His apostles and Jibreel and Meekaeel, so surely Allah is the enemy of the unbelievers.

99. And certainly We have revealed to you clear communications and none disbelieve in them except the transgressors.

100. What! whenever they make a covenant, a party of them cast it aside? Nay, most of them do not believe.

101. And when there came to them an Apostle from Allah verifying that which they have, a party of those who were given the Book threw the Book of Allah behind their backs as if they knew nothing.

102. And they followed what the Satans chanted of sorcery in the reign of Sulaiman, and Sulaiman was not an unbeliever, but the Satans disbelieved, they taught men sorcery and that was sent down to the two angels at Babylon, Harut and Marut, yet these two taught no man until they had said, “Surely we are only a trial, therefore do not be a disbeliever.” Even then men learned from these two, magic by which they might cause a separation between a man and his wife; and they cannot hurt with it any one except with Allah’s permission, and they learned what harmed them and did not profit them, and certainly they know that he who bought it should have no share of good in the hereafter and evil was the price for which they sold their souls, had they but known this.

103. And if they had believed and guarded themselves (against evil), reward from Allah would certainly have been better; had they but known (this).

104. O you (people) of Faith! Do not say Raina (to the Prophet) but (say) clearly words of respect like Unzurna; and listen carefully (to him); for those without Faith, there is a painful punishment.

105. Those who disbelieve from among the followers of the Book do not like, nor do the polytheists, that the good should be sent down to you from your Lord, and Allah chooses especially whom He pleases for His mercy, and Allah is the Lord of mighty grace.

106. Whatever communications We abrogate or cause to be forgotten, We bring one better than it or like it. Do you not know that Allah has power over all things?

107. Do you not know that Allah’s is the kingdom of the heavens and the earth, and that besides Allah you have no guardian or helper?

108. Rather you wish to put questions to your Apostle, as Musa was questioned before; and whoever adopts unbelief instead of faith, he indeed has lost the right direction of the way.

109. Many of the followers of the Book wish that they could turn you back into unbelievers after your faith, out of envy from themselves, (even) after the truth has become manifest to them; but pardon and forgive, so that Allah should bring about His command; surely Allah has power over all things.

110. And keep up prayer and pay the poor-rate and whatever good you send before for yourselves, you shall find it with Allah; surely Allah sees what you do.

111. And they say: None shall enter the garden (or paradise) except he who is a Jew or a Christian. These are their vain desires. Say: Bring your proof if you are truthful.

112. Yes! whoever submits himself entirely to Allah and he is the doer of good (to others) he has his reward from his Lord, and there is no fear for him nor shall he grieve.

113. And the Jews say: The Christians do not follow anything (good) and the Christians say: The Jews do not follow anything (good) while they recite the (same) Book. Even thus say those who have no knowledge, like to what they say; so Allah shall judge between them on the day of resurrection in what they differ.

114. And who is more unjust than he who prevents (men) from the masjids of Allah, that His name should be remembered in them, and strives to ruin them? (As for) these, it was not proper for them that they should have entered them except in fear; they shall meet with disgrace in this world, and they shall have great chastisement in the hereafter.

115. And Allah’s is the East and the West, therefore, whither you turn, thither is Allah’s purpose; surely Allah is Amplegiving, Knowing.

116. And they say: Allah has taken to himself a son. Glory be to Him; rather, whatever is in the heavens and the earth is His; all are obedient to Him.

117. Wonderful Originator of the heavens and the earth, and when He decrees an affair, He only says to it, Be, so there it is.

118. And those who have no knowledge say: Why does not Allah speak to us or a sign come to us? Even thus said those before them, the like of what they say; their hearts are all alike. Indeed We have made the communications clear for a people who are sure.

119. Surely We have sent you with the truth as a bearer of good news and as a warner, and you shall not be called upon to answer for the companions of the flaming fire.

120. And the Jews will not be pleased with you, nor the Christians until you follow their religion. Say: Surely Allah’s guidance, that is the (true) guidance. And if you follow their desires after the knowledge that has come to you, you shall have no guardian from Allah, nor any helper.

121. Those to whom We have given the Book read it as it ought to be read. These believe in it; and whoever disbelieves in it, these it is that are the losers.

122. O children of Israel, call to mind My favor which I bestowed on you and that I made you excel the nations.

123. And be on your guard against a day when no soul shall avail another in the least neither shall any compensation be accepted from it, nor shall intercession profit it, nor shall they be helped.

124. And when his Lord tried Ibrahim with certain words, he fulfilled them. He said: Surely I will make you an Imam of men. Ibrahim said: And of my offspring? My covenant does not include the unjust, said He.

125. And when We made the House a pilgrimage for men and a (place of) security, and: Appoint for yourselves a place of prayer on the standing-place of Ibrahim. And We enjoined Ibrahim and Ismail saying: Purify My House for those who visit (it) and those who abide (in it) for devotion and those who bow down (and) those who prostrate themselves.

126. And when Ibrahim said: My Lord, make it a secure town and provide its people with fruits, such of them as believe in Allah and the last day. He said: And whoever disbelieves, I will grant him enjoyment for a short while, then I will drive him to the chastisement of the fire; and it is an evil destination.

127. And when Ibrahim and Ismail raised the foundations of the House: Our Lord! accept from us; surely Thou art the Hearing, the Knowing:

128. Our Lord! and make us both submissive to Thee and (raise) from our offspring a nation submitting to Thee, and show us our ways of devotion and turn to us (mercifully), surely Thou art the Oft-returning (to mercy), the Merciful.

129. Our Lord! and raise up in them an Apostle from among them who shall recite to them Thy communications and teach them the Book and the wisdom, and purify them; surely Thou art the Mighty, the Wise.

130. And who forsakes the religion of Ibrahim but he who makes himself a fool, and most certainly We chose him in this world, and in the hereafter he is most surely among the righteous.

131. When his Lord said to him, Be a Muslim, he said: I submit myself to the Lord of the worlds.

132. And the same did Ibrahim enjoin on his sons and (so did) Yaqoub. O my sons! surely Allah has chosen for you (this) faith, therefore die not unless you are Muslims.

133. Nay! were you witnesses when death visited Yaqoub, when he said to his sons: What will you serve after me? They said: We will serve your God and the God of your fathers, Ibrahim and Ismail and Ishaq, one God only, and to Him do we submit.

134. This is a people that have passed away; they shall have what they earned and you shall have what you earn, and you shall not be called upon to answer for what they did.

135. And they say: Be Jews or Christians, you will be on the right course. Say: Nay! (we follow) the religion of Ibrahim, the Hanif, and he was not one of the polytheists.

136. Say: We believe in Allah and (in) that which had been revealed to us, and (in) that which was revealed to Ibrahim and Ismail and Ishaq and Yaqoub and the tribes, and (in) that which was given to Musa and Isa, and (in) that which was given to the prophets from their Lord, we do not make any distinction between any of them, and to Him do we submit.

137. If then they believe as you believe in Him, they are indeed on the right course, and if they turn back, then they are only in great opposition, so Allah will suffice you against them, and He is the Hearing, the Knowing.
